font-size: 10pt;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">SS chemical tankers are increasingly being used in the CPP trade. It has the following advantages---<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>No need to vent after Gasoline to desorb soft epoxy coating.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Extra tank cleaning is avoided.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Small full tanks mean less vapour growth due to sloshing and cargo loss due to higher PV valve settings OF +2000 mm Aq or more.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>No contamination claims as all tanks have their own lines.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Flexibility in loading and discharging, no stress problems in harbour condition.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Less ROB in sump after discharging.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>No salt water can be used used in SS tanks for bottom flushing , hence no fear of chloride contamination.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>No IG soot, so the empty tank after dischg can be inspected better without entry as there is no IG fog<o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>NBR seats of butterfly valves can be eaten up by gasoline in one voyage \u2014on SS chemical tankers the valves have Teflon seats. <o:p></o:p></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>More than 20 tanks ( each with its own manifold discharge pipe) --hence commingling clause avoided on B/Ladings , in case of many shippers and consignees.</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>SS ships have Nitrogen plants--hence NO soot contamination.</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 78.5pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: large;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></i><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">AVTAG or JP4 has Gasoline base and a FP of &lt;23C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">AVTUR , JET A-1 , JP-5 has Kerosene base and FP&gt;38C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">A Naphtha is sour is its Mercaptan level is &gt;100 ppm and H2S level&gt;10 ppm. Aviation fuels must not be loaded after sour cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b>LEAD</b>:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">For many cargoes including Molasses the last 3 cargoes must be lead free. Be attentive about lead content, if it is not declared in Gasoline ask for it.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Unavoidable pipeline admixture between Avgas and Mogas , in case of single connection and line, should be from a higher to lower octane number\u2014to preserve the quality of the higher grade. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">When mixing 14% nitric acid\u2014add acid to water inside tank.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Lead in leaded dyes is completely soluble in Nitric acid.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Suitable chemicals are:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Leadclean CP<b> </b>(spraying method).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Bufferclean Ph 5.5 Vecom.(Recirculation method).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp5\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Toluene and Xylene are also good solvents of lead.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Many grades of gasoline contain minute quantities of the toxic lead compounds, Tetry-Ethyl-Lead (TEL) and Tetry-Methyl-Lead (TML). Organic compounds of lead, in liquid, solid or vapor form, are highly poisonous to any living form.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Lead can be detected very easily in a lab test by change of colour, so do not take chances.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify; text-indent: -.5in;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Gasolenes contain dyes&nbsp; will turn a methanol wall wash to a pinkish color. It is very important that the dye is removed prior to loading subsequent cargo(es), since with time the dye is harder to remove. The dye can be removed by recirculating an oxidizer solution.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">JET FUEL: <o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">A SS chemical tanker carried BIODIESEL/ vegetable oil, and on the next voyage Jet A1, for the US air force , a cargo which is highly sensitive to contamination. As per the charterers instructions only a nominal wash was given. The outturn samples failed . It must be remembered that all modern fighter jets have microfilters which get choked. Vegetable oil is particularly liable to cause contamination since it is very difficult to remove it completely from tanks and piping. Contamination claims are usually huge and it also spoils the image of the company with the P&amp;I and the cargo interests. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Hot washing will not always remove residues of a solidifying cargo. Often operators load an intermediate cargo to clean the tanks which is not susceptible to contamination and which will act as a solvent. In the above case an intermediate cargo such as gas oil should have been carried. Remember the buck stops at the Masters table. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">It is a golden rule that Jet A1 should never follow a vegetable oil cargo. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div align=\"left\" class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent2\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: .5in; text-align: left;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">If manual desludging of tanks is done, the residues must be disposed of in accordance with the relevant Marpol rules.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align=\"left\" class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent2\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: .5in; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div align=\"left\" class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent2\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: .5in; text-align: left;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">SS tankers carrying CPP should top up their small tanks with extreme caution preferably loading by gravity or a centrifugal pump at low rate.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Remember after Furnace oil it is difficult to load CPP. We do not allow it unless followed by an intermediate solvent like LDO ( not golden HSD ). The Heavy oil embedded in teflon valve seatrings will keep diffusing.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">STATIC ELECTRICITY :<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Restrict initial loading rates for kerosene and jet fuels , when splashing and surface turbulence occur, to flow rates less than 1 meter/second (volume flow rate conversions tables are available in ISGOTT). Adequate inlet coverage's are: side or horizontal entrance- 0.6 meter; downward pointing inlet- twice the inlet diameter . When necessary to use inert gas to displace clean products, a minimum amount must be used, particularly for aviation fuels. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Clean product lines should never be blown with air.&nbsp; All pipes, hoses, and fittings be conductive, electrically continuous, and bonded to ship's structure. Cargo transfer piping must be insulated from the land-side terminal since electrical potential may differ from that of the vessel due to stray current or cathodic protection of the pier. Insulating flanges, joints, or sleeves are sometimes used to divide the cargo hoses into electrically isolated halves - onboard and shore side. Each half is bonded and grounded to its respective base potential.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Do not allow ship-to-shore bonding except where required by statute. In such a case, insulating flanges are still required in cargo lines. Non-conductive hose can become conductive with use and is not an acceptable substitute for an insulating flange. Insulating flanges must be used when connected to submarine pipelines which have cathodic protection.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">When doing STS electrical bonding between 2 ships is not necessary.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc3Qhbrb4I/AAAAAAAAB3w/2SFAFP6Qzdg/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc3Qhbrb4I/AAAAAAAAB3w/2SFAFP6Qzdg/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">-------CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 years in command )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-xolbu8rI/AAAAAAAABk4/84VWxVfBOBo/s1600/akash+ganga+lawn.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-xtc4onmI/AAAAAAAABk8/KgFU-uV6rkI/s1600/GOC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-xtc4onmI/AAAAAAAABk8/KgFU-uV6rkI/s1600/GOC.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-xxESn-4I/AAAAAAAABlA/lT_KgF7orK0/s1600/securedownload.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-xxESn-4I/AAAAAAAABlA/lT_KgF7orK0/s1600/securedownload.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-x0x0iVUI/AAAAAAAABlE/6RdmGbMpu2A/s1600/securedownload+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-x0x0iVUI/AAAAAAAABlE/6RdmGbMpu2A/s1600/securedownload+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Arabs called Kerala Khair Allah, the land blessed by god. The term \" Gods own country\" is derived from this.<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">However Emperor Ashoka referred to this place as Keralaputra . The state tourism department likes to say that it is because of KERA , the coconut tree.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Islam did not come here by the sword, like the rest of India , but by trade. Also Muhammad the Prophets disciple Malik Ibn Dinar had come to Kerala. This is the reason the Gulf countries love to employ , their \"once upon a time benefactors\" , the Mayaleees.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I am from the land of Kerala , on the SW coast of India , just 80 miles in width of mostly naturally reclaimed land between the western ghat mountains and the sea -- also known as gods own country or the land of plenty.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I was born in Calicut , where Vasco da Gama landed up in 1498 on Kappad beach..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">National Geographic has placed it in the top five of most beautiful spots on earth considering-- her lush landscapes with a thousand hues, idyllic backwaters , lagoons, swaying palm trees , azure blue skies, &nbsp;zephyr breezes and sun drenched golden beaches -- are a sight for the sore eyes..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Western tourists say that in Kerala they are not cheated-- probably due to the high education rate and innate intelligence.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If you visit a temple in Kerala , you are left alone. Try going to any north Indian temple, and check out how many people including Pandas ( priests ) try to fleece you.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I remember when my ship docked at Aruba, we went ashore . While driving to the Riviera past cacti dotted wilderness , my wife kept asking me , \" When are we reaching Aruba? \" . &nbsp;I said \" Baby, we are right here in Aruba. &nbsp;All they have is blue sea and white sand , &nbsp;what are your expecting? &nbsp;a super Kerala ? \" .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At home when i open the front door in the morning twilight, &nbsp;i can see hundreds of multi coloured birds, with a resounding orchestra of twitter , swooping on the flower nectar , before the crows wake up and set up a cacophony. Our door bell is a jarring electric clanging bell-- we just cant put the modern electronic sweet bird tweeters , as we get confused.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In Singapore where i stayed for 5 months, you can see swank artificial ( almost plastic ) gardens , lawns and parks without birds, bees, butterflies and squirrels. Imagine , they do manual pollination. Sorry- nature refuses to be cheated.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Many of Kerala\u2019s social indicators are the best on the planet and the state has the highest human development index in India. The people here have extraordinary political awareness , social consciousness and elected the first communist government on the planet.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Since there has been mixing of blood for centuries, some girls here are fair and far prettier and full blooded than Aishwarya Rai. Of course they would not putt micro mini chaddi and parade in front of strange males and lisp bull in a Miss World contest-- that as soon as the function is over they plan to join mother Theresa's merry band and wash the sores of them lepers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So we have an ex-tailor as our chief minister and a militant union labourer from a closed down Calicut factory Gwalior Rayons as our industries minister. A wax statue of Saddam Hussain in Trivandrum museum gets a lot of westerner tourists pissed off.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The people here are tolerant and communal riots do not happen here while the rest of India burns. Rather he will gel with another Malayali whether he is a Hindu or a Christian.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Malayalis do have attitude problems and all have a point to prove. Kerala has a remittance economy and 80% of its GDP is from workers abroad.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Survival in a lush land like Kerala is not a problem-- clothing and shelter is not an issue here. Immediately he whooped in jubilation \" This means you cant sleep under a tree !!\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There is no hero worship out here. You cant have MGRs and NTRs here.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When you see a crowd in a shamiana it could be a funeral or a wedding, unlike north India where the gleeful balle balle or woeful cries can be heard far away. So if adults especially teachers act in such a frivolous manner as in the video below, it is most unusual.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/QKDvU-YE7qc/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/QKDvU-YE7qc&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/QKDvU-YE7qc&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A lower caste Malayali will say ILLA for NO. A higher caste Malayali will say ILLYA in a rubbing it in sort of manner. So quintessential Malayalis are famous for putting Y's liberally while speaking English. I Yam what i Yam type. Palindrome MALAYALAM can be spelt both ways .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A true Malayali also cannot put his O in the proper place. So instead of saying \" my goggles are broken\" he will say \" my googles are broaken\" .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A true Malayali will use a thorthu ( guaze type absorbent bath towel ) and eat boiled rice, no matter where he stays .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Unlike the rest of India Keralites do not celebrate Diwali. Unlike the rest of India there are no clusters of houses called villages. Houses are uniformly spread all over the land--of course cities have more density. It is the only state in India where women outnumber men.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Kerala had the most rigid and mindlessly cruel caste system. The brahmin Namboodiris would keep their own women virgins ( called Antharjanams , most of them look as insipid as last nights dinner leftovers , in any case ) and would fornicate with other caste women-- by law.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Low caste women could not cover their breasts in public. Low caste people could drink tea only from coconut shell . In 1893 a daring low caste man Ayyankali ( martial art kalari expert ) was the first to break the shackles and take his bullock cart with big brass bells clanging , through a public road. He was also the first to start a school for low caste children. Mahatma Gandhi was so impressed he came all the way to Kerala to meet Ayyankali.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Here is a true joke. A namboodiri ( brahmin ) was wading though a flooded paddy field. Since lesser mortals could not step into the same water body, all were waiting for him to pass, respectfully maintaining the allowed distance. When the namboodiri saw a husband standing with his attractive wife, he hiked his mundu a wee bit upward, as a result his huge hydrocealed balls popped from underneath. He poses a loaded question to the husband -\" Ithe entha? ( what is this ? ). The man replies \" athe TRIKUNNA! ( majesty, that is your honourable nay venerable , balls )\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">Today Kerala is the least caste conscious. And poor slothful Namboodiris who had taken advantage of all since 4000 BC, because they knew Sanskrit ( high literature Malayalam is more or less Sanskrit ) , lead poverty stricken lives dreaming of past glory and hubris.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"></span>Namboodiri's and Bhattatiris' claims of superior intelligence , which they have been crying over roof tops for centuries , goes for a toss, &nbsp;as hardly a Namboodiri boy or girl passes the highly competitive IIT entrance exam. Many hundreds of years ago, the Palghat king fell in love with a low caste woman and decided to marry her. None of the Namboodiris were willing to solemnize the remony. To add injury to insult they also said if the king marries this girl, they will not do any important poojas in the temples. The king was in a bind, till he was assured secretly by the Tamilian Brahmins that they would do the ceremonies .The king got pissed off and kicked all of them out, from where they migrated to the Payyannur area. The king then invited these astute Tamilian Brahmins to Palghat who were more than happy to be amidst fantastic greenery and clean water&nbsp;&nbsp;and stay in comfortable agraharams. These are the forefathers of the Seshan types , who know how to manipulate and pull levers.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Edakkal caves in Wayanad district has rock carvings <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">12000 years</span> old. &nbsp;It contains a wheel too along with animals and birds. Very few places in the world has such old carvings.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The worlds first civilization was at the Saraswati river banks from 9000 BC to 4000 BC when the river suddenly dried up, due to tectonic shifts blocking the Himalayan glacier, making the river non-perrennial. Rig veda refers only to river Saraswati.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When the river dried up the elite migrated all over to Europe, Mesopotamia ,Russia, west coast of India till Kerala.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">During the reign of\nKing Vikramaditya in 7000 BC, the people of Kerala called Thirayyar ( sea warriors\n) did trade with the Island of Crete.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The patron saint of the\nKerala Thirayyars </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">is </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rishi Therayar , the first disciple of Maharishi\nAgastya . Agastya , the greatest of the Sapt Rishis, also famous as the first\nof the Siddhas , who also founded the Kalari Payattu art of fighting.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There\nwas a great tectonic shift and volcanic activity in 5000 BC , &nbsp;and then trade was abandoned. &nbsp;Some settled down in Judea. Today their Tantric worship forms called\nTheyyam can be seen in some temples of Kerala.</span></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Warrior saint Parashurama came from this Saraswati river banks to <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Kerala in 4100 BC</span> and reclaimed Kerala from the sea by throwing his axe as per legend. Later by 600 BC the Arabs became middlemen and monopolized the lucrative trade.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rSAhQiAItQQ/TjYwFwO5LOI/AAAAAAAAE44/g4_9mYYfWEU/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rSAhQiAItQQ/TjYwFwO5LOI/AAAAAAAAE44/g4_9mYYfWEU/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-csbrVwGW9mI/TjYwKVsWjxI/AAAAAAAAE48/x47BQoCVebY/s1600/imagesCAQ57M27.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-csbrVwGW9mI/TjYwKVsWjxI/AAAAAAAAE48/x47BQoCVebY/s1600/imagesCAQ57M27.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WEakzyJ7ZrU/TjYwO7TGNuI/AAAAAAAAE5A/YGZFPT0zVDg/s1600/imagesCANWP2YH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WEakzyJ7ZrU/TjYwO7TGNuI/AAAAAAAAE5A/YGZFPT0zVDg/s1600/imagesCANWP2YH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Arabs built their civilizations by being parasites and middlemen of Kerala goodies and mathematics \u2013 riches came pouring in. Cinnamon was more expensive than gold.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">The </span><span style=\"color: red;\">Egyptian Pharoahs wanted Malabar Cinnamon </span><span style=\"color: black;\">or Karampatta ( not lesser Cassia ) for embalming themselves after death and trade flourished. &nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">It is NO great mystery to us, who his architects were!. the great pyramid has an angle of 51 deg 49 min 38.25 sec--the same as our 6000 year old Hindu symbol Sri Yantra. &nbsp;Also why the great pyramid has the same golden pi/ phi &nbsp;ratio of 1.618033989 ( Fibonacci ratio )</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The pictures of the great Pyramid chief architect ( a man &nbsp;of highest hierarchy with the Pharoah ) are seen in British museum and in Western museums. See the picture below. Th U shape on his forehead and arms are Vaishavite ( Lord Vishnu is the protector , has it on his forehead)</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9Ki5rQGdXFA/TV6CeOO9u7I/AAAAAAAADfw/tPyP9RxDpUo/s1600/pyramid+builder.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9Ki5rQGdXFA/TV6CeOO9u7I/AAAAAAAADfw/tPyP9RxDpUo/s320/pyramid+builder.JPG\" width=\"220\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The greatest son of Kerala is Adi Sankaracharya who lived in <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">2000 BC</span>. He was a seer ,intellectual, &nbsp;philosopher, scholar and poet. He was born in Kaladi of Kerala. He mastered the Vedas written in 5000 BC, at the tender age of five. He wrote the Brahmasutra Bhasya on Upanishads and Gita.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\nTo place him later in history by 2800 years the British in\ncollusion with Tamil Iyers made a cock and bull story. That while on the banks\nof the river Narmada, he saved Guru Govinda Bhagawatpad from drowning in a\ncave, while in Samadhi. &nbsp;That a grateul Govinda initiated him into Sanyas and taught\nhim the four Mahavakyas \u2013 Tat tvamasi, Prajnanam Brahma, Aham Brahmasmi and\nAyamatma Brahma.<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br />\n<o:p></o:p></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 18px;\">The first integrator of Hindu India, he</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\">&nbsp;established four mathas ( mutts ) in four directions of the country \u2013 Jyotirmath in North, Govardhan Math at Puri in east, Shringeri Matha in Karnataka in south and Dwarika math in&nbsp;Gujarat&nbsp;in west and established Kanchi Kamakoti Peetham at Kanchi as his abode.&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 18px;\">Shankara lived for only 32 years and died at Kanchipuram. &nbsp;He also composed 240 stotras, prakaran granthas, introductory books such as .Upadesh Sahasri, Vivek Chudamani, Aparokshanubhuti etc., in all eighty books in number. All of the could speak perfect Malayalam, but still observed their customs including Sabbath and passover feast.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">By </span><span style=\"color: red;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">345 AD </span>400 Nasrani Syrian Christians landed here </span><span style=\"color: black;\">for refuge in 3 ships along with Mar Joseph\u2014 a bishop and settled down a Kodungalloor... till the Portugese destroyed their settlements.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">In <span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">520AD</span>,</span> Bodh Dharma taught the Chinese Kungfu-- our 6000 year olf martial art Kalari.</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/sbWuk5AjHhg/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/sbWuk5AjHhg&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/sbWuk5AjHhg&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\nIn<span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red;\"> 643 AD </span>, the favourite disciple of Mohammed the Prophet, &nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">Malik-Ibn -Dinar</span> came to Calicut , with&nbsp;a letter from Kerala King Cheraman Peruman who went to see the uncle of Mohammed ( the priest&nbsp; from his Calicut court -&nbsp; who was in charge of the Shiva temple at Mecca Oasis and his in-charge at the&nbsp;&nbsp;trading post to Jerusalem/ Petra&nbsp;)&nbsp;, and uncle of Mohammed . Cheraman died on his way back and his body is buried at Salalah , Oman.&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cheraman met Mohmmed too, as per Ibn Batuta's accounts. </span><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ibn Battuta </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">was a Moroccan traveller who was a Qazi at the Calicut King's court in </span><span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">1344 AD&nbsp;.</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n<br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red;\">In 1433 AD</span> the great <span style=\"color: red;\">Chinese Admiral Zheng He</span> dies in Calicut. His tomb was destroyed by the British -not-- the Portuguse. His fleet had Chinese junk ships, 600 feet long &nbsp;10 times the size of Vasco da Gama's ships. He made 7 trips to Calicut. This is why in several ancient tharavadus in Calicut there are Ming Lanterns, still looking brand new.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">Columbus sailed out from Huelva for Calicut and instead lost his way and discovered America.</span><span style=\"color: red;\"> In <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">1498 AD</span> Vasco da Gama landed at Kappad beach.</span><span style=\"color: black;\"> He thought of bowling over the sophisticated Malayalees who wore silk diamonds, and gold with coloured glass and beads, like how he impressed the ignorant blacks of Africa, and came a cropper . </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><em>Glass HA-- wrong number !  Ancient Indian Vimanas as per Vimanaka Shastra of 5000 BC had heat resistant sodalime glass containers to hold mercury . Our Mahabharata wax palace of 4000 BC, where Draupadi made fun of Duryodhana , had transparent glass windows. The Univeristy of Taxila of 3000 BC had a text Vedic text Shatapata Brahmana . This university had <span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">10500 seats for world students were available as long as they were more than the age of 16. Students came from as far as Mesopotamia, Greece, Syria, Arabia , Russia, Thailand and China. Our ancient kings placed water filled globe glasses to magnify written texts.</span></em></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">India was the only source of diamonds on this planet from 150 years ago.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Little did he know that when the white man lived in caves, doing grunt grunt for speech , wore hides and ate raw meat, these people live in pucca stone houses , wrote poems , wore silk n diamonds and ate cooked delicacies from a menu . He introduced Pirangi Punnu ( foreign sore ) or Syphilis to Kerala.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Vasco da Gama's soldiers started stealing Pepper vines and secreted it away on their ships for planting it in Portugal. He died of Malaria and was first buried at Kochi for 15 years.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">In <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">1542</span> St Francis Xavier was busy with the Paravar community ( pearl divers ) trying to convert them to Christianity</span><span style=\"color: black;\">. font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u092a\u0930\u0902</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u0927\u0930\u094d\u092e\u092e\u0947\u0915\u0902</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u0938\u0926\u093e</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u092e\u093e\u0928\u092f\u093e\u092e\u0903</span><o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u092a\u094d\u0930\u093f\u092f\u0902</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u092d\u093e\u0930\u0924\u0902</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u0924\u0924\u094d</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u0938\u0926\u093e</span>&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\">\u0935\u0928\u094d\u0926\u0928\u0940\u092f\u092e\u094d</span><o:p></o:p><br /><span style=\"font-family: mangal, serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-size: 17.6px;\">\nWe bow to the land, to India,<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px;\">\nThe one supreme dharma, we always esteem,<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px;\">\nFor which we offer our wealth, our life,</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px;\">\nBeloved India, always to be respected<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; clear: both; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; BHAVA&nbsp; RAGA- TALA .<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/N9wulkyMbNQ/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/N9wulkyMbNQ&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/N9wulkyMbNQ&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "51", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/857412378129300095/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "5964592483081813743", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-08T21:03:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-12-14T15:16:17+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkyMzE5OTc3MzY5Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/pigging-on-chemical-tankers-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/5964592483081813743", "title": "PIGGING ON CHEMICAL TANKERS -  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">PIPELINE PIGGING CHEMICAL TERMINALS</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-kzqeQMRI/AAAAAAAABkI/x6goq3-FZ9U/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-kzqeQMRI/AAAAAAAABkI/x6goq3-FZ9U/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-k7p_4guI/AAAAAAAABkQ/E3UjFC_v03c/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-k7p_4guI/AAAAAAAABkQ/E3UjFC_v03c/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">A pig is a rubber sphere or cylinder pushed trough the shore pipeline by compressed air ( 40 to 100 psi ) or propelled by another grade of liquid.&nbsp; The pig catcher is a pig receiver which is mounted outboard of the ships manifold, from which the pig may be removed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">At some terminals the shore pipeline from shore tanks to ships manifold is pigged. Its is possible that a large amount of cargo enters the tank at a very fast rate and high pressure. The amount which comes in must be discussed in the preloading meeting . Precautions must betaken by chief officer to prevent a spill on board.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Clearing line without pig\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The manifold valve is closed at the completion of the loading operation and is not opened until the commencement of the line clearing operation.&nbsp; At the beginning of the line clearing operation, the pump stack or tank valve is partly opened. Then the manifold valve is opened and manually throttled (opened and closed repeatedly) to control the operation.&nbsp; The valve operator needs to listen for the sound of flowing cargo or gas in the line, and close the valve when a flow of gas is heard. An experienced operator should be in control of the valve during the line clearing operation. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The operator in control of the manifold valve must maintain direct communication with dock personnel during the entire line clearing operation. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The manifold valve is throttled in short bursts during the line clearing operation to facilitate the clearing process and to control the pressure in the tank.&nbsp; The manifold valve should never be fully opened.&nbsp; Between bursts of compressed gas, the pressure in tank should be allowed to equalize/dissipate.&nbsp; The type of manifold valve being used has a significant impact on the quality of control during the line clearing operation. Ball and gate valves are more effective than butterfly valves when attempting to manually control the flow rate of compressed gas. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Lifting hoses, tapping lines, and feeling for \u201chot\u201d cargo are methods used to indicate how well the line clearing operation is proceeding.&nbsp; The pressure in the line must be allowed to \u2018bleed off\u2019 prior to disconnecting hoses. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\">In no case should the P/V vents be restricted or closed while line clearing to the vessel. </span><b><o:p></o:p></b></span></div><div class=\"CM6\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM6\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Line Clearing with pig-- <o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-lA7rZwvI/AAAAAAAABkU/6BTUAq-_JHU/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-lA7rZwvI/AAAAAAAABkU/6BTUAq-_JHU/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"CM6\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Procedures must be in place to ensure the correct pig (type and size) is used. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The system should be lined up with the vessel manifold valve closed.&nbsp; Responsible personnel should verify the lineup and ensure that all safeguards are operational. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The pig should be introduced at the pig launcher.&nbsp; Care must be taken to ensure that the pig is properly positioned in the launcher.&nbsp; The pressure should be equalized between the line and the pig launcher.&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: windowtext;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The vessel should open it\u2019s manifold valve part way.&nbsp; Compressed gas should be introduced into the launcher, behind the pig, to begin moving the pig through the line. Personnel should monitor the flow of cargo and the movement of the pig throughout the operation and communicate this information to each other.&nbsp; Once the pig enters the pig trap, the shore valve and vessel manifold valve should be closed immediately.&nbsp; The line and hoses from shore to vessel manifold should then be cleared directly as described previously.&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"Default\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc85FhaUYI/AAAAAAAAB5U/PUF9ELSn9O0/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc85FhaUYI/AAAAAAAAB5U/PUF9ELSn9O0/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-k2ayrnzI/AAAAAAAABkM/m_IyQH_mmhk/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TP-k2ayrnzI/AAAAAAAABkM/m_IyQH_mmhk/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">..<o:p></o:p></span></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
